          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/2021/3/2/22309176/fox-news-dr-seuss-cancel-culture-fox-news-biden">
            Why Fox News is having a day-long meltdown over Dr. Seuss
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           Biden didnt mention Dr. Seuss in his Read Across America Day statement. All hell broke loose from there.
          </p>

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/2021/3/2/22309326/supreme-court-voting-rights-act-brnovich-democratic-national-committee-carvin-brett-kavanuagh">
            The Voting Rights Act had a surprisingly good day at the Supreme Court
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">

         <div class="c-entry-box--compact__body">
          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/2021/3/2/22309042/biden-russia-sanctions-alexei-navalny">
            US to sanction Russian officials over the attempted murder of Alexei Navalny
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           The sanctions put the US in line with actions taken by the European Union and United Kingdom last year.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline">
           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">
            By
            <span class="c-byline__item">
             <a data-analytics-link="author-name" href="https://www.vox.com/authors/alex-ward">
              <span class="c-byline__author-name">
               Alex Ward
              </span>
             </a>
            </span>

           </a>

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/recode/22308263/youtube-google-land-of-the-giants-podcast">
            How YouTube swallowed the world
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           Googles video site has room for everything, from everyone. Is that a feature or a bug?
          </p>

    <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
     (function(){
  // load outbrain js
  function loadOutbrain(){
    var ref = document.querySelector("div.OUTBRAIN");

    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.setAttribute('type','text/javascript');
    script.setAttribute('src', 'https://widgets.outbrain.com/outbrain.js');
    script.setAttribute('async', 'async');

    ref.appendChild(script);
  }

  // Disable on mobile and tablet screens
  // 880px is the upper bound for the `medium` breakpoint defined in UserAgent JS lib.
  var shouldDisable = false && screen.width <= 880;
  var scrollSubscriber = document.cookie.indexOf("scroll0=") > -1;
  var hymnalPreviewContent = !!(window.location.href.indexOf("concert_preview") > -1);

  if (!shouldDisable && !scrollSubscriber && !hymnalPreviewContent) {
    // first, set a timeout to loadOutbrain, in case no ads load in 5s
    // (i.e., blocked). once an ad has loaded, create a new timeout that
    // will load outbrain if openmic doesn't get loaded in 2s
    //
    var adBlockerTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 5000);
    document.body.addEventListener('first_ad_rendered', function(){
      clearTimeout(adBlockerTimeoutId);
      var outbrainTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 2000);
      document.body.addEventListener('playlistRendered', function(){
        clearTimeout(outbrainTimeoutId);
      });
    });
  }
})();
    </script>
